[维权网：中国大陆1666名在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引（2023年12月31日）（第99期）](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/16662023123199.html)
------

<div>
<p><span></span></p><a name='more'></a><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;"><br /></span><p></p><p><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">为了更方便人们查询本网统计的在押政治犯、良心犯的名单，本网每期随《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》一起发布《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》。本索引将本期报告所统计的人员名单，以人员姓名拼音字母排序（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">A</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">B</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">C</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">D</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">E</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">F.....X</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">Y</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">Z</span><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12pt;">）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。</span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt;">如您获知有未上名单的政治犯良心犯的境况，请随时向我们知会，联系邮箱：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">名单索引如下</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">A.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布杜热扎克•夏木西丁（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布拉江·阿乌提·阿有普（<span lang="EN-US">Ablajan Awut Ayup</span>）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿尔恒•巴杂尔别克（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;
